Combine

Combine country with release_year by adding pattern " - " in between two strings.

df_5<-df
df_5$country_release_year<-paste(df_5$country,df_5$release_year, sep=" - ")

Split OR Truncate

Split listed_in by pattern " , " (i.e. split the characters whenever , is encountered).

df_6<-df
slist<-str_split(string = df_6$listed_in,pattern = "[,]")

Code<-data.frame((Reduce(rbind,slist)))

df_6<-cbind(df_6,Code)
rownames(df_6) <- NULL

Or Truncate show_id in a way that only the numbers are displayed. Note that all records have the same “sxx” structure and length.

df_7<-df_4
list<-str_sub(string = df_7$show_id,start=2,end=5)
id<-data.frame((Reduce(rbind,list)))
df_7<-cbind(df_7,id)
rownames(df_7) <- NULL

df_7<-df_7%>%rename(id=X.Reduce.rbind..list..)
